    <script data-n-head="ssr" data-pbody="true">
    "use strict";
    (function() {
        var n = "themeMode",
            o = ["theme-mode-dark", "theme-g100"],
            l = ["theme-mode-light", "theme-g10"];
        function t(a) {
            document.body.classList.add.apply(document.body.classList, a === "dark" ? o : l),
            document.body.classList.remove.apply(document.body.classList, a === "dark" ? l : o)
        }
        function r(a) {
            let i = document.body.parentElement;
            i && (i.style.colorScheme = a)
        }
        var s = "(prefers-color-scheme: dark)",
            c = window.matchMedia(s),
            h = c.media === s,
            e = null;
        try {
            e = localStorage.getItem(n)
        } catch {}
        var m = e !== null;
        if (m && (e = JSON.parse(e)), m)
            t(e),
            r(e);
        else if (h) {
            var d = c.matches ? "dark" : "light";
            t(d),
            r(d)
        } else
            t("light"),
            r("light")
    })();
    </script>

                                                                                                                    </svg>
                                                                                                                </span>

                                                                                                        <section id="simulators-overview">
                                                                                                            <span id="system-backends-simulators"></span>
                                                                                                            <h1>
                                                                                                                Simulators overview
                                                                                                                <a class="headerlink" href="#simulators-overview" title="Permalink to this heading">¶</a>
                                                                                                            </h1>
                                                                                                            <nav class="contents local" id="contents">
                                                                                                                <ul class="simple">
                                                                                                                    <li>
                                                                                                                        <p>
                                                                                                                            <a class="reference internal" href="#overview" id="id6">Overview</a>
                                                                                                                        </p>
                                                                                                                    </li>
                                                                                                                    <li>
                                                                                                                        <p>
                                                                                                                            <a class="reference internal" href="#statevector" id="id7">Statevector</a>
                                                                                                                        </p>
                                                                                                                    </li>
                                                                                                                    <li>
                                                                                                                        <p>
                                                                                                                            <a class="reference internal" href="#stabilizer" id="id8">Stabilizer</a>
                                                                                                                        </p>
                                                                                                                    </li>
                                                                                                                    <li>
                                                                                                                        <p>
                                                                                                                            <a class="reference internal" href="#extended-stabilizer" id="id9">Extended stabilizer</a>
                                                                                                                        </p>
                                                                                                                    </li>
                                                                                                                    <li>
                                                                                                                        <p>
                                                                                                                            <a class="reference internal" href="#mps" id="id10">MPS</a>
                                                                                                                        </p>
                                                                                                                    </li>
                                                                                                                    <li>
                                                                                                                        <p>
                                                                                                                            <a class="reference internal" href="#qasm" id="id11">QASM</a>
                                                                                                                        </p>
                                                                                                                    </li>
                                                                                                                </ul>
                                                                                                            </nav>
                                                                                                            <section id="overview">
                                                                                                                <span id="id1"></span>
                                                                                                                <h2>
                                                                                                                    Overview
                                                                                                                    <a class="headerlink" href="#overview" title="Permalink to this heading">¶</a>
                                                                                                                </h2>
                                                                                                                <p>
                                                                                                                    IBM Quantum features a collection of high-performance 
                                                                                                                    <a class="reference external" href="../../terms-glossary#term-simulator">simulators</a>

                                                                                                                    for prototyping 
                                                                                                                    <a class="reference external" href="../../terms-glossary#term-quantum-circuit">quantum circuits</a>
                                                                                                                     and algorithms, and exploring their
                                                                                                                    performance under realistic device 
                                                                                                                    <a class="reference external" href="https://qiskit.org/documentation/apidoc/aer_noise.html">noise models</a>
                                                                                                                    .
                                                                                                                </p>
                                                                                                                <p>
                                                                                                                    To view available simulators, on the upper left corner of the screen,  click the Application switcher ( 
                                                                                                                    <img alt="switcher" src="https://iqx-docs.quantum-computing.ibm.com/iql/manage/simulator/../../../_images/switcher-small2.png">
                                                                                                                     ), select 
                                                                                                                    <strong>Compute resources</strong>
                                                                                                                      to view the 
                                                                                                                    <a class="reference external" href="https://quantum-computing.ibm.com/services/resources?services=simulators">Compute resources page,</a>
                                                                                                                     then click the Simulators tab.
                                                                                                                </p>
                                                                                                                <p>
                                                                                                                    The default choice of simulator should be the 
                                                                                                                    <code class="docutils literal notranslate">
                                                                                                                        <span class="pre">simulator_statevector</span>
                                                                                                                    </code>
                                                                                                                     as it is a general-purpose solution method.
                                                                                                                    The following simulation methods are currently available, and support a maximum of
                                                                                                                    300 circuits and 8192 shots per job.
                                                                                                                </p>
                                                                                                                <div class="instructions admonition">
                                                                                                                    <p class="admonition-title">Simulator timeout limit</p>
                                                                                                                    <p>To prevent the simulators from processing jobs that would otherwise not finish processing
                                                                                                                    in a reasonable amount of time, jobs sent to the simulators are limited to run
                                                                                                                    times under 10,000 seconds (~2.75 hours).</p>
                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                            </section>
                                                                                                            <section id="statevector">
                                                                                                                <span id="id2"></span>
                                                                                                                <h2>
                                                                                                                    Statevector
                                                                                                                    <a class="headerlink" href="#statevector" title="Permalink to this heading">¶</a>
                                                                                                                </h2>
                                                                                                                <div class="line-block">
                                                                                                                    <div class="line">
                                                                                                                        <strong>Type:</strong>
                                                                                                                         Schrödinger wavefunction
                                                                                                                    </div>
                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                <div class="line-block">
                                                                                                                    <div class="line">
                                                                                                                        <strong>Name:</strong>
                                                                                                                         simulator_statevector
                                                                                                                    </div>
                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                <p>Simulates a quantum circuit by computing the wavefunction of the qubit’s
                                                                                                                statevector as gates and instructions are applied. Supports general
                                                                                                                noise modeling.</p>
                                                                                                                <div class="docutils container">
                                                                                                                    <div class="column-50 docutils container">
                                                                                                                        <p>
                                                                                                                            <strong>Qubits:</strong>
                                                                                                                             32 
                                                                                                                            <span class="raw-html">
                                                                                                                                <br>
                                                                                                                            </span>
                                                                                                                            <strong>Noise modeling:</strong>
                                                                                                                             Yes
                                                                                                                        </p>
                                                                                                                    </div>
                                                                                                                    <div class="column-50 docutils container">
                                                                                                                        <p>
                                                                                                                            <strong>Supported gates / instructions</strong>
                                                                                                                        </p>
                                                                                                                        <div class="highlight-python notranslate">
                                                                                                                            <div class="highlight">
                                                                                                                                <pre>
                                                                                                                                    <span></span>
                                                                                                                                    <span class="p">[</span>
                                                                                                                                    <span class="s1">'u1'</span>
                                                                                                                                    <span class="p">,</span>
                                                                                                                                    <span class="s1">'u2'</span>
                                                                                                                                    <span class="p">,</span>
                                                                                                                                    <span class="s1">'u3'</span>
                                                                                                                                    <span class="p">,</span>
                                                                                                                                    <span class="s1">'u'</span>
                                                                                                                                    <span class="p">,</span>

                                                                                                                                    <span class="s1">'rx'</span>

                                                                                                                                    <span class="s1">'cu1'</span>

                                                                                                                                    <span class="s1">'cu2'</span>

                                                                                                                                    <span class="s1">'rzx'</span>

                                                                                                                    </div>
                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                            </section>
                                                                                                            <section id="stabilizer">
                                                                                                                <span id="id3"></span>
                                                                                                                <h2>
                                                                                                                    Stabilizer
                                                                                                                    <a class="headerlink" href="#stabilizer" title="Permalink to this heading">¶</a>
                                                                                                                </h2>
                                                                                                                <div class="line-block">
                                                                                                                    <div class="line">
                                                                                                                        <strong>Type:</strong>
                                                                                                                         Clifford
                                                                                                                    </div>
                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                <div class="line-block">
                                                                                                                    <div class="line">
                                                                                                                        <strong>Name:</strong>
                                                                                                                         simulator_stabilizer
                                                                                                                    </div>
                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                <p>An efficient simulator of Clifford circuits. Can simulate noisy
                                                                                                                evolution if the noise operators are also Clifford gates.</p>
                                                                                                                <div class="docutils container">
                                                                                                                    <div class="column-50 docutils container">
                                                                                                                        <p>
                                                                                                                            <strong>Qubits:</strong>
                                                                                                                             5000 
                                                                                                                            <span class="raw-html">
                                                                                                                                <br>
                                                                                                                            </span>
                                                                                                                            <strong>Noise modeling:</strong>
                                                                                                                             Yes (Clifford only)
                                                                                                                        </p>
                                                                                                                    </div>
                                                                                                                    <div class="column-50 docutils container">
                                                                                                                        <p>
                                                                                                                            <strong>Supported gates / instructions</strong>
                                                                                                                        </p>
                                                                                                                        <div class="highlight-python notranslate">
                                                                                                                            <div class="highlight">
                                                                                                                                <pre>
                                                                                                                                    <span></span>
                                                                                                                                    <span class="p">[</span>
                                                                                                                                    <span class="s1">'cx'</span>

                                                                                                            <section id="extended-stabilizer">
                                                                                                                <span id="extended"></span>
                                                                                                                <h2>
                                                                                                                    Extended stabilizer
                                                                                                                    <a class="headerlink" href="#extended-stabilizer" title="Permalink to this heading">¶</a>
                                                                                                                </h2>
                                                                                                                <div class="line-block">
                                                                                                                    <div class="line">
                                                                                                                        <strong>Type:</strong>
                                                                                                                         Extended Clifford (e.g., Clifford+T)
                                                                                                                    </div>
                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                <div class="line-block">
                                                                                                                    <div class="line">
                                                                                                                        <strong>Name:</strong>
                                                                                                                         simulator_extended_stabilizer
                                                                                                                    </div>
                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                <p>Approximates the action of a quantum circuit using a ranked-stabilizer
                                                                                                                decomposition.  The number of non-Clifford gates determines the number
                                                                                                                of stabilizer terms.</p>
                                                                                                                <div class="docutils container">
                                                                                                                    <div class="column-50 docutils container">
                                                                                                                        <p>
                                                                                                                            <strong>Qubits:</strong>
                                                                                                                             63 
                                                                                                                            <span class="raw-html">
                                                                                                                                <br>
                                                                                                                            </span>
                                                                                                                            <strong>Noise modeling:</strong>
                                                                                                                             No
                                                                                                                        </p>
                                                                                                                    </div>
                                                                                                                    <div class="column-50 docutils container">
                                                                                                                        <p>
                                                                                                                            <strong>Supported gates / instructions</strong>
                                                                                                                        </p>
                                                                                                                        <div class="highlight-python notranslate">
                                                                                                                            <div class="highlight">

                                                                                                                <h2>
                                                                                                                    MPS
                                                                                                                    <a class="headerlink" href="#mps" title="Permalink to this heading">¶</a>
                                                                                                                </h2>
                                                                                                                <div class="line-block">
                                                                                                                    <div class="line">

                                                                                                                    </div>
                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                <div class="line-block">

                                                                                                                        <strong>Name:</strong>

                                                                                                                    </div>
                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                <p>A tensor-network simulator that uses a Matrix Product State (MPS)
                                                                                                                representation for the state that is often more efficient for states
                                                                                                                with weak entanglement.</p>

                                                                                                                    <div class="column-50 docutils container">

                                                                                                                <h2>
                                                                                                                    QASM
                                                                                                                    <a class="headerlink" href="#qasm" title="Permalink to this heading">¶</a>
                                                                                                                </h2>
                                                                                                                <div class="line-block">
                                                                                                                    <div class="line">
                                                                                                                        <strong>Type:</strong>
                                                                                                                         General, context-aware
                                                                                                                    </div>

                                                                                                                <div class="line-block">

                                                                                                                        <strong>Name:</strong>
                                                                                                                         ibmq_qasm_simulator
                                                                                                                    </div>
                                                                                                                </div>
                                                                                                                <p>A general-purpose simulator for simulating quantum circuits both ideally
                                                                                                                and subject to noise modeling.  The simulation method is automatically
                                                                                                                selected based on the input circuits and parameters.</p>
